unki pehali home production film 'chote nawab' thi
 He made the suspense-comedy film Bhoot Bangla as a director
 abhinayta, nirdeshak, kathakaar or nirmaataa ke rup main kaam karne vaale mahmud ne shahrukh khan ko lekar varsh 1996 main apni aakhri film 'dushman duniya kaa' banaai, lekin vah box offis par naakaam rahi
 To avoid uniformity in his image, Mahmood introduced himself in a wide variety of roles
 isi kram main varsh 1968 main film 'padosan' kaa naam sabase pehle aata he
 In 'padosan', Mahmood played a negative role and managed to rob the applause of the audience
 'padosan' 60 ke dashak kii jabardast hit sabit hui thi
 'padosan' is counted among the best comedy films of the Hindi cinema world
 apni anek filmon main vah nayak ke kirdaar par baari najar aae
 The song 'ek Chatur Nar Karkar Shringar', which was filmed on Mehmood in 'padosan', became very popular
 1970 main film 'hamajoli' main mahmud ke abhinay ke vividh rup darshakon ko dekhne ko mili
 In this film, Mahmood played a triple role and caught the attention of the audience
 tippaniyan Mehmood was awarded the Filmfare Award thrice in his cine career
 23 july, 2004 ko mahmud is duniya se hameshaa ke liye chale gaye or hamaare bich keval unki khubasurat yaaden hi baaki hai
 (this news has not been edited by the NDTV team
 yah syndicate feed se sidhe prakashit kii gai he
 ) mahmud kii bhashaa main hyderaabadi andaaj darshakon ko behad pasand aayaa or unke bolne kii kala or abhinay ke laajawab andaaj ne karodon logon ko apana divaana bana liya
 At the time when Mahmud started taking films seriously, Kishore Kumar's comedy was overshadowed in the Indian film industry
 lekhak manmohan melville ne apane ek lekh main mahmud or kishor ke dilachasp kisse ko bayaan kiya he
 It said that Mahmood had requested Kishore, who is going through the golden phase of his career, to play a role in one of his films, but Kishore, who was fully aware of Mahmood's talent, said that how can he give such a chance to someone Which will become a challenge for them in the future
 is par mahmud ne badi vinamrata ke saath kaha ki ek din main bhi bada filmkaar banuunga or aapako apni film main bhoomika duungaa
 Mehmood proved his point and later when he started his home production film 'padosan', he hired Kishore in it
 in donon mahaan kalakaaron kii jugalbandi se yah film bollywood kii sabase badi kamedi film sabit hui
 He has more than 300 Hindi films in Mahmood's three-decade long career
 mahmud abhinayta or nrity kalakaar mumtaj ali ke aath bacchon main se ek the
 Prior to his work as an actor, he used to do petty jobs, also driving vehicles
 us jamaane main minaa kumari ko teble tennis sikhaane ke liye unhen naukari par rakhaa gaya tha
 He later married Meena Kumari's sister Madhu
 shaadi karne or pita banane ke baad zyada paise kamaane ke liye unhone abhinay karne kaa nishchay kiya
 Initially, he played minor roles in films like 'do Bigha Zameen' and 'pyaasa'
 mahmud ko filmon main pehla bada mauka 'parvarish' (1958) se mila tha
 In this, he played the role of the brother of the film's hero Raj Kapoor and after that he also acted in the film 'gumnaam'
 unhone 'pyaar kiye ja', 'pyaar hi pyaar', 'sasuraal', 'lav in tokyo' or 'ziddee' jaisi hit filmein di
 He then went on to play the lead role in a few films, but the audience liked him more as a comedian
 mahmud ne baad main apana khud kaa production house kholaa
 His first home production film was 'chhote Nawab'
 unhone bataur nirdeshak suspence-kamedi film 'bhoot bangla' banaai
 Mahmood, who worked as an actor, director, narrator and producer, made his last film 'dushman Duniya Ka' in 1996 with Shah Rukh Khan, but failed at the box office
 apni chhavi main ai ekarupata se bachane ke liye mahmud ne apane aap ko vibhinn prakaar kii bhoomikaaon main pesh kiya
 In the same sequence, in the year 1968, the name of the film 'padosan' comes first
 'padosan' main mahmud ne nakaaratmak bhoomika nibhaai or darshakon kii vaahvahee luutane main safal rahe
 'padosan' was a tremendous hit of the 60s
 'padosan' ko hindi cinema jagat kii shreshth hasya filmon main gina jaataa he
 He appeared heavily on the character of the hero in many of his films
 'padosan' main mahmud par filmaaya gaanaa 'ek chatur naar karke shringaar' kaaphi lokapriy hua
 In the 1970 film Humjoli, the audience got to see various forms of acting of Mahmood
 is film main mahmud ne tihari bhoomika nibhaai or darshakon kaa dhyaan apni ore khinchaa
 The comments mahmud ko apane sine kariyar main teen baar filmphere puraskaar se sammanit kiya gaya
 On 23 July 2004, Mahmud departed from this world forever and only his beautiful memories remain among us
 (is khabar ko enditivi team ne sampadit nahin kiya he
 It is published directly from the Syndicate feed
 ) Writer Manmohan Melville has narrated an interesting anecdote of Mahmood and Kishore in one of his articles
 isamen kaha gaya he ki mahmud ne apane kariyar ke sunahare daur se guzar rahe kishor se apni kisi film main bhoomika dene kii guzarish kii thi, lekin mahmud kii pratibha se puri tarah waakif kishor ne kaha tha ki vah aise kisi vyakti ko mauka kaise de sakate hai, jo bhavishya main unheen ke liye chunauti ban jaae
 On this, Mahmud said with great humility that one day i will also become a big filmmaker and will give you a role in my film
 mahmud apni baat ke pakke sabit hue or aage chalakar jab unhone apni home production kii film 'padosan' shuru kii to usamen kishor ko kaam diya
 The film proved to be Bollywood's biggest comedy film due to the jugalbandi of both these great actors
 mahmud ke teen dashak lambey kariyar main 300 se zyada hindi filmein unke naam hai
 Mahmood was one of the eight children of actor and dance artist Mumtaz Ali
 abhinayta ke taur par kaam se pehle vah chote-mote kaam karte the, vaahan chalaane kaa kaam bhi karte the
 At that time, Meena Kumari was hired to teach table tennis
 baad main unhone minaa kumari kii bahan madhu se shaadi kii
 After marrying and becoming a father, he decided to pursue acting to earn more money
 shuruyaat main unhone 'do bigha jameen' or 'pyaasa' jaisi filmon main chote-mote kirdaar nibhaae
 Mehmood got his first big chance in films with 'parvarish' (1958)
 isamen unhone film ke nayak rajkpur ke bhai kaa kirdaar nibhaayaa tha or uske baad unhone film 'gumnaam' main bhi kaam kiya
 He gave hits like 'pyar Kiya Jaa', 'pyar Hi Pyar', 'sasural', 'love in Tokyo' and 'stubborn'
 iske baad unhone kuch filmon main mukhya bhoomika bhi nibhaai, lekin darshakon ne unhen ek kamedian ke taur par zyada pasand kiya
 Mahmud later opened his own production house
 unki pehali home production film 'chote nawab' thi
 He made the suspense-comedy film Bhoot Bangla as a director
 abhinayta, nirdeshak, kathakaar or nirmaataa ke rup main kaam karne vaale mahmud ne shahrukh khan ko lekar varsh 1996 main apni aakhri film 'dushman duniya kaa' banaai, lekin vah box offis par naakaam rahi
 To avoid uniformity in his image, Mahmood introduced himself in a wide variety of roles
 isi kram main varsh 1968 main film 'padosan' kaa naam sabase pehle aata he
 In 'padosan', Mahmood played a negative role and managed to rob the applause of the audience
 'padosan' 60 ke dashak kii jabardast hit sabit hui thi
 'padosan' is counted among the best comedy films of the Hindi cinema world
 apni anek filmon main vah nayak ke kirdaar par baari najar aae
 The song 'ek Chatur Nar Karkar Shringar', which was filmed on Mehmood in 'padosan', became very popular
 1970 main film 'hamajoli' main mahmud ke abhinay ke vividh rup darshakon ko dekhne ko mili
 In this film, Mahmood played a triple role and caught the attention of the audience
 tippaniyan Mehmood was awarded the Filmfare Award thrice in his cine career

 unki har adaa kaatilaanaa thi

 unase pehle ke star raaj kapur or dilip kumaar ke liye bhi log pagal rahete the lekin is baat main koi shaq nahin ki jo deewangi rajesh khanna ke liye thi, waisi pehle yaa baad main kabhi nahin dikhi
 Rajesh Khanna was born on 29 December 1942 in Amritsar and was raised by his adoptive parents
 unka naam pehle jatin khanna tha
 Rajesh Khanna had an inclination towards acting since school days and due to this he acted in many plays
 sapanom ke pankh lagane kii umr aayi to jatin ne filmon kii raah pakadaney kaa faisla kiya

 is naam ne na keval unhen shoharat di balki yah naam har yuvak or yuvati ke zehan main amar ho gaya

 unki sabase pehali film ‘aakhri khat’ thi jise chetan anand ne nirdeshit kiya tha

 yah film bhi pratiyogita jeetne kaa hi puraskaar thi

 rajesh khanna ne ‘bahaaron ke sapane’, ‘aurat’, ‘doli’ or ‘ittefaq’ jaisi shuruaati safal filmein deen lekin 1969 main aayi ‘aradhana’ ne bollywood main ‘kaaka’ ke daur kii shuruyaat kar di

 ‘aradhana’ film se kishor kumaar jaise gayak ko bhi hindi film jagat main khud ko sthapit karne kaa mauka mila or antat: vah rajesh khanna ke geeton kii sthaayee aawaaj ban gaye

 'aradhana' and 'haathi Mere Saathi' were Rajesh Khanna's super hit films that broke all the previous records of success at the box office
 unhone 163 filmon main kaam kiya jinamein se 106 filmon ko unhone sirf apane dam par safalataa pradaan kii

 phir chaahe ve film nideshak rahe hon yaa abhinetriyaan or sangeetkaar

 Many times you buy a second hand mobile from the shop or from an acquaintance, but later you have to regret it because its features are not as per your expectation
 aise main phone khareednaa ghate kaa sauda sabit hota he
 Let us tell you about some things that you should keep in mind before buying an old phone
 jisase aap dhokhe or nuksaan se batch saken
 1
 phone charchingmobile kharidne ke baad zyaadaatar logon kii samasya phone charching ko lekar hi hoti he
 So whenever you go to buy a phone, take a USB cable with you
 isse aap data transfar ke saath-saath betry sahi tareeke se charge ho rahi he yaa nahin iskaa bhi pataa laga paaenge
 2
 camera ficharsasmartphone rakhane waalon zyaadaatar logon ko photo khichne kaa shauk hota he
 In such a situation, before buying another phone, please check his camera
 saath hivideo banakarbhi dekh len
 Many times the camera features look fine on the screen, but after dragging the photos the quality is quite poor
 isliye rier camera, front camera or flash sabhi ko achche se check kar lenaa chahie
 3
 celular networkkoi purana phone kharidne se pehle celular network ke bare main jaankaree le len
 Sometimes a device supports only one or two cellular networks
 aisa aksar un smartphone ke saath hota he jinhen videshon se laayaa jaataa he
 That is why it is necessary to check the call out going and speakers with the network connection
 kai baar network conection sho karne ke baad bhi divaais se kol nahin lagati he
 Doing so will check the phone's speaker, connection and phone's mic
 4
 IMEI number Dial * # 06 # on the phone and try to mix the IMEI number of your handset and the number written on the battery
 agar donon alag hai to bydaree badali gai he
 In such a situation, the user can also give you a local battery of poor quality by deception
 5
 Connectivity featurestechnical disturbances At times, gadgets include blu-tooth, wi-fi and other connectivity options stop working
 koi bhi purana phone lene se pehle ye dhyaan rakhen ki bluetooth, vaai-faai, yuasabi jaise connactivity opshan thik se kaam kar rahe hai yaa nahin
 6
 phone kaa displepurane phone kii sabase badi kharabi hoti he phone kaa disple, jiske kharaab hone kaa khatra sabase zyada hota he
 If you see a spot of black-colored color anywhere on the screen, then it is a dead pixel, it must be checked before purchasing the phone
 saath hi dekh len ki sabhi batan achche se kaam kar rahe hai yaa nahin
 7
 memory stateskisi bhi second hand mobile ko kharidte samay phone kaa memory states jarur check kar len
 For this, you can try to shift any file from internal memory to external memory
 agar file aasaani se transfar ho rahi he to thik he, varanaa phone main koi pareshaani he

 2 kilometre ke daayre ko paryaavaran ke lihaaj se atisamvedansheel ghoshit karne ko kaha
 Now the decision of the NGT is that the dreams of about twenty five thousand people in Noida have come true
 sanyukt pragatisheel gathbandhan (samprag) evam congress adhyaksh sonia gandhi ne yahaan shanivaar ko kattarpanthi ugravadi sanghathanon se apil kii ki ve centre sarkaar ke shanti prastaav par amal karen or rajya ko vikaas ke path par le jane main sahyog den
 In a large public meeting organized to mark the completion of one year of the third term of the Congress government led by Chief Minister Tarun Gogoi, Sonia said, “I am very happy to see the changed picture of the state
 " Sonia arrived here despite the proclamation of the anti-peace negotiation group led by Paresh Barua of the militant group ULFA (united Liberation Front of Assam)
 band kaa elaan unke daure ke virodh main kiya gaya he
 The same group had detonated a bomb in Tinsukia district on Friday night, in which one person was killed
 sonia ne kade suraksha prabandhon ke bich yahaan ke sarusojaai stadium ke ek badi jansabha ko sambodhit kiya
 The ceremony was organized at the same stadium on the first anniversary of the Congress government in the state
 congress yahaan lagaataar teesri baar satta main ai he
 Sonia said, "I am very happy to be here today
 yah bahut sukhad avasar he kyonki congress ke netritv main lagaataar teesri baar gathit sarkaar ne ek saal puraa kar liya he
 "he said that this is an indication that the policies of the government have been able to win the trust of the people of the state
 logon ke vishwaas ne sarkaar kii jimmedaariyaan badha di hai
 Sonia said, "most militant organizations have agreed that violence will not solve their problems
" main ummid karti hum ki jo log shanti samjhaute se abhi tak duuri banaae hue hai, ve bhi centre sarkaar kii shanti pahal main bahut jald shaamil ho jaaenge
 "he said," You all know that when the Congress government was formed in 2001 under the leadership of Chief Minister Tarun Gogoi, the state of the state was extremely miserable
 sarkari karmchaariyon ko vetan nahin mil rahaa tha
 There were no roads, no rural development programs and industries
 kanoon evam vyavastha kii samasya ke chalate vyavsaayee rajya ko chhodane lage the
 Today i am very happy to see the changed picture here
 "tippaniyan The Congress president said, "about 27 years ago, the former Prime Minister late Rajiv Gandhi signed the historic Assam Accord for the development of the state
 maujuuda sarkaar rajya ko vikaas kii ore le jane ke liye lagaataar assam samjhaute ke nirdesh ke mutabik kaary kar rahi he
 "he said," It is the result of the continuous efforts of the current government that the state has been able to achieve many achievements in terms of development
 assam ne khadyannon kaa ricard utpaadan kar desh main ek itihaas rachaa he
 The tea industry has received a life lease during the last 11 years of Congress rule in Assam
 assam aisa pehla rajya he jahaan ucch vidyalayon ke chaatro ko muft commuter die gaye hai
 " sonia ne kaha, "rajya ke logon ne sarkaar ko harasambhav sahyog diya he or congress sarkaar assam ko desh ke viksit evam shantipurna rajyon main se ek banane kii prakriya main logon ko kabhi niraash nahin hone degi
 " mukhyamantri tarun gogoi ke netritv vaali congress sarkaar ke tisare kaarykaal ke ek varsh puraa hone ke avasar par yojit ek badi jansabha main sonia ne kaha, "main rajya kii badali hui tasviir dekhakar behad khush hum
 " sonia ugravadi sanghathan ulpha (united libration front of assam) ke paresh barua ke netritv vaale shanti vaarta virdohi gut ke band ke elaan ke baavjood yahaan pahunchin
 The bandh was announced to protest against his visit
 isi gut ne shuukravaar raat tinsukiya jile main ek bam visphot kiya tha, jisamen ek vyakti kii maut ho gai thi
 Sonia addressed a large public meeting at the Sarsuzai Stadium here amidst tight security arrangements
 rajya main congress sarkaar kii pehali varshganth par samaaroh kaa aayojan isi stadium main kiya gaya
 Congress has come to power for the third time in a row
 sonia ne kaha, "main aaj yahaan aakar behad khush hum
 This is a very happy occasion as the government constituted for the third consecutive time under the leadership of the Congress has completed one year
 " unhone kaha ki yah is baat kaa sanket he ki sarkaar kii nitiyaan rajya ke logon kaa vishwaas jeetne main sakasham rahi hai
 The trust of the people has increased the responsibilities of the government
 sonia ne kaha, "zyaadaatar ugravadi sanghathan yah maan chuke hai ki hinsa se unki samasyaon kaa hal nikalne vaala nahin he
 i hope that those who have stayed away from the peace agreement will join the Central Government's peace initiative very soon
 " unhone kaha, "aap sabhi ko pataa hi he ki 2001 main jab mukhyamantri tarun gogoi ke netritv main congress kii sarkaar bani thi, us samay rajya kii sthiti atyant shochaneey thi
 Government employees were not getting salary
 sadaken nahin thim, koi gramin vikaas kaarykram or udyog nahin tha
 Due to law and order problem, businessmen started leaving the state
 aaj main yahaan kii badali hui tasviir dekhakar bahut khush hum
 "comments congress adhyaksh ne kaha, "lagbhag 27 varsh pehle purv pradhanmantri swargeey rajeev gandhi ne rajya ke vikaas ke liye aitihaasik assam samjhaute par hastakshar kiye the
 The present government is continuously working as per the instructions of the Assam Accord to take the state towards development
 " unhone kaha, "yah maujuuda sarkaar ke nirantar prayaason kaa hi parinaam he ki rajya ne vikaas ke maamle main kai uplabdhiyaan hasil karne main sakasham rahi he
 Assam has created a history in the country by producing a record of food grains
 chaay udyog ko assam main congress shashan ke pichley 11 varshon ke dauraan aaajeevan patta mila he
 Assam is the first state where free commuters have been provided to students of high schools
 " Sonia said, "the people of the state have given all possible support to the government and the Congress government will never let people down in the process of making Assam one of the developed and peaceful states of the country
